楷体_GB2312;color:black'>D.</span><span lang="EN-US" style='mso-bidi-font-size:

<p align="left" class="MsoNormalCxSpLast" style="text-align:left;line-height:150%"><u><span lang="EN-US" style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif";

<p align="left" class="MsoNormalCxSpFirst" style="text-align:left;line-height:150%"><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:black'>已知集合</span><i style="mso-bidi-font-style:normal"><span lang="EN-US" style='mso-bidi-font-size:
10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif";color:black'>M</span></i><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:black'>中的元素</span><i style="mso-bidi-font-style:normal"><span lang="EN-US" style='mso-bidi-font-size:

"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:black'>是</span><span lang="EN-US" style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Cambria Math","serif";
mso-bidi-font-family:"Cambria Math";color:black'>△</span><i style="mso-bidi-font-style:

"Times New Roman";color:black'>一定不是（</span><span lang="EN-US" style='mso-bidi-font-size:

color:black'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:150%"><span lang="EN-US" style='mso-bidi-font-size:
10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif";color:black'>A</span><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:black'>．锐角三角形</span><span lang="EN-US" style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif";

<p class="MsoNormal"><i style="mso-bidi-font-style:normal"><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri">【解析】</span><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p align="left" class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="text-align:left;line-height:
150%"><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:楷体_GB2312;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
color:black'>因为集合中元素具有互异性，所以</span><i style="mso-bidi-font-style:normal"><span lang="EN-US" style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:楷体_GB2312;color:black'>a</span></i><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:楷体_GB2312;

color:black'>，</span><i style="mso-bidi-font-style:normal"><span lang="EN-US" style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:楷体_GB2312;color:black'>b</span></i><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:楷体_GB2312;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
color:black'>，</span><i style="mso-bidi-font-style:normal"><span lang="EN-US" style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:楷体_GB2312;color:black'>c</span></i><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:楷体_GB2312;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
color:black'>互不相等，因此选</span><span lang="EN-US" style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;
line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif";mso-fareast-font-family:

<p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:left;line-height:150%"><u><span lang="EN-US" style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif";

<p align="left" class="MsoNormalCxSpFirst" style="text-align:left;line-height:150%"><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:black'>已知集合</span><i style="mso-bidi-font-style:normal"><span lang="EN-US" style='mso-bidi-font-size:

"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:black'>中的元素</span><i style="mso-bidi-font-style:normal"><span lang="EN-US" style='mso-bidi-font-size:

10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif";color:black'>A</span><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

<h6><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:
major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin">【解析】</span></h6>
<p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:left;line-height:150%"><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:楷体_GB2312;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
color:black'>因为集合中元素具有互异性，所以</span><i style="mso-bidi-font-style:normal"><span lang="EN-US" style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif";

<h6><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:

<p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:left;line-height:150%"><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:楷体_GB2312;

color:black'>因为集合中元素具有互异性，所以</span><i style="mso-bidi-font-style:normal"><span lang="EN-US" style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:楷体_GB2312;color:black'>a</span></i><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:楷体_GB2312;

color:black'>，</span><i style="mso-bidi-font-style:normal"><span lang="EN-US" style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:楷体_GB2312;color:black'>b</span></i><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:楷体_GB2312;

color:black'>，</span><i style="mso-bidi-font-style:normal"><span lang="EN-US" style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif";
mso-fareast-font-family:楷体_GB2312;color:black'>c</span></i><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:楷体_GB2312;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
color:black'>互不相等，因此选</span><span lang="EN-US" style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;
line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif";mso-fareast-font-family:
楷体_GB2312;color:black'>D.</span><span lang="EN-US" style='mso-bidi-font-size:
10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif";color:black'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<h6><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:
